<!\[CDATA\[ IT Business Analyst – SharePoint & RFP Consultant \]\]>**IT Business Analyst – SharePoint & RFP Consultant (Contract)**

**Location:**

Ottawa, ON – **Hybrid (3 days on-site/week preferred, 1 day remote possible)**

**Overview:**

Our client is seeking a highly skilled **IT Business Analyst – SharePoint & RFP Consultant** to support the development of a formal Request for Proposal (RFP) for a SharePoint Online implementation. This consultant will serve as the subject matter expert in SharePoint functionality, working closely with senior stakeholders, procurement specialists, and cross-functional teams to define project requirements and ensure an RFP that aligns with strategic goals and compliance standards.

**Key Responsibilities:**

**RFP Development**

- Lead the creation of a clear, structured RFP outlining:
- Project objectives
- Scope
- Functional and technical requirements
- Timelines, challenges, and budget estimates

Ensure training requirements are included for administrators, IT staff, and end users
Collaborate with the procurement team to integrate our client’s terms, controls, schedules, and workflows**Requirements Gathering & Stakeholder Engagement**
- Review existing documentation (e.g., risk assessments, third-party reports, executive briefings)
- Facilitate and document stakeholder interviews with Directors, VPs, and SMEs across departments including:
- Operations, Security, IT, Communications, Major Projects, Finance
Define and validate project scope, specifying inclusions/exclusions
Ensure consistent communication and consensus across all internal groups**SharePoint Capabilities Alignment**

- Translate SharePoint Online capabilities into functional business requirements
- Assess and prioritize features to be included in the RFP:
- Intelligent Intranet & Digital Workplace
- Document Management
- Workflow Automation
- Microsoft 365 Integration
- Governance & Compliance
- Secure External Collaboration
- Analytics & Continuous Improvement
- Low-Code/No-Code Development
- Change Enablement

**Evaluation & Compliance**

- Partner with procurement to define evaluation criteria for vendor selection
- Ensure all RFP elements are aligned with procurement policies and regulatory guidelines

**Quality Assurance**

- Review and refine all RFP content for clarity, accuracy, and professionalism
- Support finalization of the RFP alongside the Director and Procurement team

**Additional Duties**

- Act as a convenor, bringing stakeholders and ideas together to drive consensus
- Perform related tasks necessary to support successful delivery of the RFP

**Required Qualifications:**

- 7+ years of experience in IT Business Analysis, preferably in the public or government sector
- Proven **functional SharePoint Online experience**

\]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Senior Manager, Radio System Engineering \]\]>As the Senior Manager of Radio System Engineering, you will lead all technical aspects of radio system architecture, including air interface definition, concept of operations, functional specifications, and physical implementation of RF functions. You will define the functional and performance requirements for the radio system across the satellite payload, user terminals, and ground infrastructure.

* * *

**Main Responsibilities:**

- Provide expert-level leadership in RF system development, including trade-offs involving ACP, PAR, out-of-band emissions, pass-band ripple, group delay, and more.

- Support the finalization of radio system implementation involving agile multi-beam phased array antennas and beam hopping technology.

- Define operational concepts for all phases of the system lifecycle such as user terminal commissioning, network entry, satellite handovers, time synchronization, and adaptive coding and modulation (ACM).

- Act as the principal architect for defining air interfaces between user terminals, ground infrastructure, and satellite payloads.

- Collaborate with RF, antenna, system, and terminal engineers to partition functionality between hardware and software components.

- Provide input to the system modeling team on design assumptions and strategies for modeling link performance, accounting for impairments across system components.

- Work closely with the Verification and Test team to ensure thorough validation of requirements and system performance.

- Participate in relevant industry standards forums (e.g., DVB) and provide strategic recommendations to align internal systems with evolving standards.


* * *

**Education & Experience – Required:**

- Bachelor’s degree in Electrical, Computer, or Systems Engineering.

- 15+ years of experience in RF communications systems and/or RF equipment development.

- Demonstrated experience taking RF systems from concept through iterative design, specification development, and low-rate production.

- Strong background in system architecture, requirements management, and performance assessment for communication systems.


* * *

**Education & Experience – Assets:**

- Familiarity with DVB standards such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2.

- Solid understanding of digital communications, spread spectrum techniques, single and multi-carrier modulation (e.g., PSK, APSK, QAM).

- Proficiency in MATLAB or equivalent tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems.

- Deep knowledge of RF passive and active components and microwave frequency performance, including the effects of environmental factors such as rain fade.

- Strong foundation in RF transceiver architecture and digital communication theory.

- Excellent communication skills, with the ability to effectively engage stakeholders across engineering, management, and external partners.

- Collaborative, adaptable, and capable of leading multidisciplinary teams in high-performance environments.


\]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Senior IAM Consultant \]\]>**Must Haves:**

·Minimum 7 years’ experience as a solution Architect on Oracle Identity Access Management systems, 10G, 11G and 12C.

·Minimum 7 years solution development with 12C OIG (Oracle Identity Governance) who has successfully migrated user, service enrolment and organization data from 10G to 12C.

·Minimum 5 years in setting up 11G OIM and 12C OIG in multi-data center configuration and set-up.

**Background Information**

Ontario Health’s ONEID service is a secure identity solution leveraged by the Ministry of Health and Long-Term Care and numerous health care organizations in Ontario for purposes of accessing patient health information (PHI). The ONEID service enhances protection of PHI and user account information through privacy and security safeguards while providing access to multiple digital health services using the same login credentials.

The ONE ID service is based on Oracle Identity Access Management suite including Oracle Access Manager (OAM), Oracle Unified Directory (OUD), Oracle Identity Management (OIM), Oracle database, Microsoft Active Directory, and other Ontario Health custom systems. As such, Ontario Health requires Oracle Access Manager (OAM) and Oracle Unified Directory (OUD) experts to help resolve and navigate challenges in configuring and setting up the new 12C OAM and OUD to establish interoperability with the existing 10G based ONE ID and provide a smooth transition to the upgraded our current 10G/11G systems including Oracle Identity Manager (OIM) and Oracle Virtual Directory (OVD) to the full Oracle 12C IAM suite.

The purpose of this procurement is to procure one (1) Senior Identity Access Management Consultant required to perform the role of 12C Oracle Identity Management (OIM) Data Migration – IAM Technical Consultant within a dedicated team for the ONEID Oracle 12c Upgrade.

**Must haves:**

· Minimum 7 years’ experience as a solution Architect on Oracle Identity Access Management systems, 10G, 11G and 12C.

· Minimum 7 years solution development with 12C OIG (Oracle Identity Governance) who has successfully migrated user, service enrolment and organization data from 10G to 12C.

· Minimum 5 years in setting up 11G OIM and 12C OIG in multi-data center configuration and set-up.

· Minimum 7 years integration experience in Oracle IAM suite including OAM, OIM, OUD/OVD, Oracle HTTP Server (OHS), Microsoft AD, and Oracle databases.

· Over 5 years of experience in tuning Oracle IAM suites to work efficiently with high availability to work on WebLogic and Linux.

· Experience on design and creation of service sand applications for enrollment in 12C OIG using native interface

· Experience in configuration of connectors and discounted resources for service/application enrollments in 12C OIG

· Must be associated with a recognized Gold Oracle IAM Partner.

· Must be at expert level in Security Assertion Mark-up Language, SMAL 2.0, and OAuth 2.0.

· Experience translating conceptual to logical to physical application architecture in alignment with business and architecture.

· Able to articulate technical issues and provide options to resolve them clearly and concisely.

· Able to produce clear and concise documentation including design/architecture documents, deployment and integration guides, and physical application design documents.

**Responsibilities:**

· Work with Ontario Health (OH) teams in design and configuration of 12C OIG in Multi-Data Centre (MDC) setup for high availability in upper and lower environments

· Work with Ontario Health (OH) teams to integrate 12C Phase 1 MDC system to existing 10G ONE ID for interoperability in environments for user and service transitions

· Work with Ontario Health (OH) teams to create and maintain service/application in 12C OIG

· Develop the flow for enrollment for each service/application

· Document the final design, installation, configuration, and integration procedures for all environments

· Work with Applications and Architects team to resolve the cross-domain and remaining 12C issues (such as the return URL) with Oracle and team.

· Work collaboratively with other Ontario Health teams such as database, networking, and infrastructure.

· Provide weekly updates to team leads and project manager.

**Desired Skills:**

· Experience with Oracle and Identity and Access Management Suite Plus and Microsoft Active Directory Suite

· Knowledge of general IAM best practises

· Experience integrating business applications with Oracle IAM and Microsoft Active Directory Suite

· Experience triaging, analyzing, diagnosing (trouble-shooting), evaluating options, and resolving application problems, especially those related to identity and access management systems

· Experience with developing user identity, service creation and enrolments with Oracle Identity Manager (OIM) and Governance (OIG).

· Knowledge of IT security technologies particularly encryption and authentication technologies such as PKI, PKI, and TLS/SSL

· Excellent organizational skills, verbal and written communication skills, team working skills

· Experience with Oracle Identity Management data migration

· Experience in working with Agile development and Continuous Integration (CI)/ Continuous Development (CD) pipelines

· Knowledge of JIRA and Confluence

· Work collaboratively:

o with internal and external stakeholders to understand Integration needs across Ontario Health and the broader health sector

o with other domain Architects as well as privacy, security and policy areas as required

o with solution vendors and/or development groups to ensure solutions conform to integration architecture

o with external organizations (e.g.: Ministry of Health, Canada Health Infoway, etc.) to ensure alignment

**Required Experience / Evaluation Criteria:**

1. Minimum 7 years’ experience as a solution Architect on Oracle Identity and Access Management systems, 10G 11G and 12C, who has successfully modeled and implemented end-to-end solutions and infrastructure.: 20 Points
2. Minimum 7 years solution development with 12C, and overall 3+ years with 12C OIG in multi-data center configuration and set-up to achieve high-availability and high performance.: 20 Points
3. Must be associated with a recognized Gold Oracle IAM Partner for over 7 years.: 20 Points
4. Hands-on 10G OIM to 12C OIG data migration experience.: 20 Points
5. Must know 12C OIG user, service creation, service enrolment and organization management.: 20 Points

Total Capabilities Evaluation Criteria: 100 Points

**Deliverables include, but are not limited to:**

· Data migration from existing 10G OIM to 12C OIG.

· Configuration of 12C OIG for service creation and enrollment.

· Integration of 12C OIM to other IAM components including 12C OAM, 12C OUD, MS AD, and Oracle database 19C.

· Design and development of a reliable and repeatable method to promote 12C OIG configuration from one environment to another.

· All design and implementation documents for the above tasks.

**Knowledge Transfer Details:**

**Configuration Identification**

- Support and coordinate activities to establish rules for configuration item (CI) selection and baseline content definition.

- Assist in selecting configuration items at appropriate levels of the product structure, including determining required configuration documentation for each CI.

- Define, develop, and manage processes, procedures, and tools to identify, document, and control physical assets for a large-scale communications system.

- Provide support for export control compliance processes such as ITAR.

- Maintain an inventory of system assets (hardware).

- Control and document system, hardware, and software configurations, including both "as-designed" and "as-built" baselines.


**Software Configuration Management – Release Monitoring**

- Collaborate with technical teams and project management to define roles and responsibilities for configuration and release management.

- Work with development, test environment, and verification teams to define and document processes for managing software releases.

- For each release, verify required documentation is complete, approved, and captured, and ensure release packages are created in accordance with established procedures.

- Confirm that pending or outstanding changes do not impact planned test or release activities.

- Support development, lab, and test teams to ensure timely and accurate release execution.

- Assist with impact assessments and update the CI Tree and related configuration documentation to reflect approved changes.

- Support preparation and execution of configuration item status accounting and configuration audits.

- Provide subject matter expertise on configuration management (CM) processes, standards, and systems.

- Contribute to requirements management and traceability process documentation and improvement.

- Develop training materials for CM identification, software/release management, and general CM procedures.

- Participate in continuous improvement initiatives to enhance CM process efficiency, reliability, and cost-effectiveness.


**Document and Library Management Support**

- Initiate updates to documentation based on approved change requests.

- Collaborate with document management personnel to track and complete implementation of documentation updates.

- Ensure all released documents are logged, captured, and statused in the document management system.

- Act as backup support for document management responsibilities when needed.

- Bachelor’s or college degree in engineering, science, or a related field (or equivalent combination of education and experience).

- 2+ years of experience in configuration and/or data management.

- 2+ years of experience in release management.

Analyzes business processes; elicits, analyzes, and documents business requirements; identifies alternative solutions, assesses feasibility and makes recommendations typically seeking to exploit and leverage new or existing technology components.

Translates business requirements into functional requirements; performs data and process modeling; manages change; and leads, coordinates / performs testing, verification, and validation of requirements.

**Job Responsibilities:**

- Elicits and communicates the organization’s business strategy; works directly with business unit clients to understand specific business processes and needs and opportunities for improvement; identifies IT capabilities and information required to support the business processes and collaborates in the development of appropriate information management strategies, developing them as an integrated part of the business strategy.
- Responsible for compliance with applicable Corporate and Divisional Policies and procedures.
- Identifies current and emerging business needs and evaluates alternative technology solutions using standard information systems methodologies and best practices.
- Proactively seek out strategic business opportunities with business unit executives for the application of new or existing technology capabilities.
- Develops technology strategies that meet the requirements of the business. Identifies the business benefits of alternative strategies. Ensures compliance between business
- strategies and technology directions. Prepares testing plans to confirm that requirements and system design are accurate and complete.
- Conducts training. Identify process disconnects and translate them into improvement opportunities with cost savings or avoidance, productivity improvements, or revenue generating business benefits. Develops business relationships and integrates activities with other BTO's to ensure successful implementation and support of project eIorts.
- Manages relationships between clients involved and BTOs to assure eIective communication between the groups is occurring. Brokers services within BTS community on behalf of customers; coordinates system solutions.
- Allies with other BTS functional areas to remain current on project status, and inform customer management of progress; conversely, keeps BTS managers aware of user issues and resolves conflicts.
- Identifies the impact of any relevant statutory, internal or external regulations on the organization's use of information.
- Exercises considerable latitude in determining objectives of assignment. Has defined authority and responsibility for a significant area of work, including technical, financial and quality aspects. Establishes organizational objectives and delegates assignments.
- Accountable for actions and decisions taken by self and subordinates.
- Accountable for the accuracy of the fit of the proposed solution to the business needs and the information upon which the business justification and prioritization decisions are made. Also accountable for communicating the business need and drivers to development groups to assure the implementation phase can fulfill the business need.

\]\]><!\[CDATA\[ Technical Support and Customer Service Associate \]\]>COLLEGIS CUSTOMER SERVICE ASSOCIATE (CSA) JOB DESCRIPTION

Position Summary:

The Customer Service Associate serves as the front line to the PSC. They are actively fielding calls, emails and chats with a goal of exceeding established service level agreements. Customer Service Associate will perform first level problem determination and troubleshooting as well as attempt to implement a resolution. If additional access or a higher level of knowledge about the environment is required to implement a solution the Tier 1 agent will utilize appropriate escalation processes to transition the caller to the correct path for resolution of their reported concern. Customer Service Associate is managed on their performance, customer service, and continued commitment to success and learning. Customer Service Associate will be granted access to a comprehensive knowledgeable base to assist them with resolution of problems as well as various training sessions to attend.

In addition to Telephone Support, Customer Service Associate will also help support customers through Chat and Email Mediums simultaneously. The support department runs 24x7x365 and Customer Service Associate may work varied shifts that could include nights, weekends, and holidays. Assignments of duties and daily tasks can change on a regular basis and focus can be reflected in a change in accounts supported.

Primary Responsibilities, Essential Functions and Requirements:

Communication & Professionalism:

The Customer Service Associate’s role is one that supports various clientele in technical and non-technical scenarios. Maintaining excellent customer service and professional communication is critical to the success of individuals within this position.

Be accountable for seeing assigned cases and tasks to completion by providing detailed documentation all details and troubleshooting steps taken for each support request to eliminate repetitive steps.

Triage with upper level agents to determine appropriate case resolution measures and implementation of solutions.

Ensure professional and respectful communication is maintained in all interactions including face to face, over the phone, via email, and chat correspondences.

Teamwork & Collaboration:

Teamwork and collaboration with PSC employees and outside departments are critical elements to being successful within the PSC. The Customer Service Associate is a focal point for all inbound activities and it is critical to convey and maintain a collaborative environment to ensure the support requests are resolved in a proper and positive manner. It is of utmost importance that PSC staff members maintain a reassuring and positive atmosphere for the caller.

Proactively work with PSC employees and PSC Leadership to better understand supported environments as well as fostering a collaborative partnership.

Work with Technical Support Analysts as well as other departments to escalate support requests in the event that a resolution cannot be found at the Customer Service Associate level.

Focus on the understanding of as well as meeting and exceeding customer service level agreements and customer satisfaction ratings.

Work with PSC Leadership to implement new initiatives and practice coaching requests.

Maintain an active approach to utilizing the Wiki and suggest updates when necessary. Consult Technical Support Analyst, Technical Service Solutions Specialist or leadership when discrepancies are found so corrections and additional research may be put forth to better the tools utilized within the PSC.

Participate in Technical Support Analyst mentoring program and perform peer assigned mentoring of Technical Support Analyst agents.

Continued development of knowledge and utilization of PSC support tool sets.

Commitment to Learning:

The PSC is a place in which systems and support models rapidly change. Support topics can vary on a day-to-day basis but can include PC & MAC troubleshooting (Hardware, Software, Network Connectivity, etc.), assisting with navigation and proper function of a Learning Management System (Online School Environment), as well as other current and future topics that will be introduced on a consistent basis. Being able to quickly learn these environments and manage the day-to-day variance is critical. Following and participating in the development of internal Personal Support Center policies and procedures will ensure a consistent approach to case management.

Take advantage of knowledge sharing sessions, online knowledge bases, standard operating procedures, and communication with other departments. Complete a minimum of 3 training sessions per quarter.

Collaboration with PSC Leadership to suggest updates to department Knowledge Base (Wiki)

Commitment to reviewing all training communications, coaching opportunities, as well as continual review and reflection upon all PSC information content sources. <!\[CDATA\[ Senior Manager, Radio System Engineering \]\]>

<description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <p>As the Senior Manager of Radio System Engineering, you will lead all technical aspects of radio system architecture, including air interface definition, concept of operations, functional specifications, and physical implementation of RF functions. You will define the functional and performance requirements for the radio system across the satellite payload, user terminals, and ground infrastructure.</p> <hr> <p><strong>Main Responsibilities:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Provide expert-level leadership in RF system development, including trade-offs involving ACP, PAR, out-of-band emissions, pass-band ripple, group delay, and more.</p> <li> <p>Support the finalization of radio system implementation involving agile multi-beam phased array antennas and beam hopping technology.</p> <li> <p>Define operational concepts for all phases of the system lifecycle such as user terminal commissioning, network entry, satellite handovers, time synchronization, and adaptive coding and modulation (ACM).</p> <li> <p>Act as the principal architect for defining air interfaces between user terminals, ground infrastructure, and satellite payloads.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with RF, antenna, system, and terminal engineers to partition functionality between hardware and software components.</p> <li> <p>Provide input to the system modeling team on design assumptions and strategies for modeling link performance, accounting for impairments across system components.</p> <li> <p>Work closely with the Verification and Test team to ensure thorough validation of requirements and system performance.</p> <li> <p>Participate in relevant industry standards forums (e.g., DVB) and provide strategic recommendations to align internal systems with evolving standards.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Required:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Bachelor’s degree in Electrical, Computer, or Systems Engineering.</p> <li> <p>15+ years of experience in RF communications systems and/or RF equipment development.</p> <li> <p>Demonstrated experience taking RF systems from concept through iterative design, specification development, and low-rate production.</p> <li> <p>Strong background in system architecture, requirements management, and performance assessment for communication systems.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Assets:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Familiarity with DVB standards such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2.</p> <li> <p>Solid understanding of digital communications, spread spectrum techniques, single and multi-carrier modulation (e.g., PSK, APSK, QAM).</p> <li> <p>Proficiency in MATLAB or equivalent tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems.</p> <li> <p>Deep knowledge of RF passive and active components and microwave frequency performance, including the effects of environmental factors such as rain fade.</p> <li> <p>Strong foundation in RF transceiver architecture and digital communication theory.</p> <li> <p>Excellent communication skills, with the ability to effectively engage stakeholders across engineering, management, and external partners.</p> <li> <p>Collaborative, adaptable, and capable of leading multidisciplinary teams in high-performance environments.</p> </ul> \]\]>

The ONEID service enhances protection of PHI and user account information through privacy and security safeguards while providing access to multiple digital health services using the same login credentials. </span></span></span><br> <span style="font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Aptos , sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10.0pt;"> The ONE ID service is based on Oracle Identity Access Management suite including Oracle Access Manager (OAM), Oracle Unified Directory (OUD), Oracle Identity Management (OIM), Oracle database, Microsoft Active Directory, and other Ontario Health custom systems. <!\[CDATA\[ <p>As an RF Systems Engineer, you will be responsible for simulating and modeling terrestrial and in-orbit communication systems. <description>

<!\[CDATA\[ <strong>COLLEGIS CUSTOMER SERVICE ASSOCIATE (CSA) JOB DESCRIPTION</strong><br> Position Summary:<br> <br> The Customer Service Associate serves as the front line to the PSC. They are actively fielding calls, emails and chats with a goal of exceeding established service level agreements. Customer Service Associate will perform first level problem determination and troubleshooting as well as attempt to implement a resolution. If additional access or a higher level of knowledge about the environment is required to implement a solution the Tier 1 agent will utilize appropriate escalation processes to transition the caller to the correct path for resolution of their reported concern. Customer Service Associate is managed on their performance, customer service, and continued commitment to success and learning. Customer Service Associate will be granted access to a comprehensive knowledgeable base to assist them with resolution of problems as well as various training sessions to attend.<br> <br> In addition to Telephone Support, Customer Service Associate will also help support customers through Chat and Email Mediums simultaneously. The support department runs 24x7x365 and Customer Service Associate may work varied shifts that could include nights, weekends, and holidays. Assignments of duties and daily tasks can change on a regular basis and focus can be reflected in a change in accounts supported.<br> <br> Primary Responsibilities, Essential Functions and Requirements:<br> <br> Communication & Professionalism:<br> <br> The Customer Service Associate’s role is one that supports various clientele in technical and non-technical scenarios. Maintaining excellent customer service and professional communication is critical to the success of individuals within this position.<br> <br> Be accountable for seeing assigned cases and tasks to completion by providing detailed documentation all details and troubleshooting steps taken for each support request to eliminate repetitive steps.<br> Triage with upper level agents to determine appropriate case resolution measures and implementation of solutions.<br> Ensure professional and respectful communication is maintained in all interactions including face to face, over the phone, via email, and chat correspondences.<br> <br> Teamwork & Collaboration:<br> <br> Teamwork and collaboration with PSC employees and outside departments are critical elements to being successful within the PSC. The Customer Service Associate is a focal point for all inbound activities and it is critical to convey and maintain a collaborative environment to ensure the support requests are resolved in a proper and positive manner. It is of utmost importance that PSC staff members maintain a reassuring and positive atmosphere for the caller.<br> <br> Proactively work with PSC employees and PSC Leadership to better understand supported environments as well as fostering a collaborative partnership.<br> Work with Technical Support Analysts as well as other departments to escalate support requests in the event that a resolution cannot be found at the Customer Service Associate level.<br> Focus on the understanding of as well as meeting and exceeding customer service level agreements and customer satisfaction ratings.<br> Work with PSC Leadership to implement new initiatives and practice coaching requests.<br> Maintain an active approach to utilizing the Wiki and suggest updates when necessary. Consult Technical Support Analyst, Technical Service Solutions Specialist or leadership when discrepancies are found so corrections and additional research may be put forth to better the tools utilized within the PSC.<br> Participate in Technical Support Analyst mentoring program and perform peer assigned mentoring of Technical Support Analyst agents.<br> Continued development of knowledge and utilization of PSC support tool sets.<br> <br> Commitment to Learning:<br> <br> The PSC is a place in which systems and support models rapidly change. Support topics can vary on a day-to-day basis but can include PC & MAC troubleshooting (Hardware, Software, Network Connectivity, etc.), assisting with navigation and proper function of a Learning Management System (Online School Environment), as well as other current and future topics that will be introduced on a consistent basis. Being able to quickly learn these environments and manage the day-to-day variance is critical. Following and participating in the development of internal Personal Support Center policies and procedures will ensure a consistent approach to case management.<br> <br> Take advantage of knowledge sharing sessions, online knowledge bases, standard operating procedures, and communication with other departments. Complete a minimum of 3 training sessions per quarter.<br> Collaboration with PSC Leadership to suggest updates to department Knowledge Base (Wiki)<br> Commitment to reviewing all training communications, coaching opportunities, as well as continual review and reflection upon all PSC information content sources. Such as Wiki, SharePoint, and other department websites. \]\]>

...

<!\[CDATA\[ <p><strong>Senior Technical NetSuite Architect</strong><br /> <strong>Part-Time Contract \| 20–30 Hours/Week \| Remote (U.S.-based only)</strong></p> <p><strong>Myticas Consulting</strong> is seeking a <strong>Senior Technical Architect</strong> with deep <strong>NetSuite ERP</strong> experience to support a long-term consulting engagement for a client in the advanced manufacturing space. This role will focus on architecting an ERP system for a network of pilot plants, helping lay the foundation for scalable and compliant manufacturing operations.</p> <h3><strong>Key Responsibilities:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Gather and document business and technical requirements.</p> </li> <li> <p>Guide ERP implementation partner selection.</p> </li> <li> <p>Architect and oversee the design of a NetSuite ERP solution aligned with manufacturing needs.</p> </li> <li> <p>Serve as a technical advisor throughout the implementation.</p> </li> <li> <p>Collaborate with both internal teams and third-party vendors.</p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong>Qualifications:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>8+ years in ERP architecture, with hands-on NetSuite experience.</p> </li> <li> <p>Strong understanding of manufacturing and supply chain workflows.</p> </li> <li> <p>Experience working with implementation partners and cross-functional teams.</p> </li> <li> <p>Excellent communication skills.</p> </li> <li> <p>Must be located in the U.S.</p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong>Preferred:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Background in biotech, industrial manufacturing, or regulated industries.</p> </li> <li> <p>Familiarity with compliance and data security best practices.</p> </li> </ul> <p><strong>Apply today</strong> to connect with our team and learn more about this exciting opportunity.</p> \]\]>
